< Text>
I can say that place was real nice but thats kind of brought down by average mall goers walking in with flip flops and gym clothes. I'm not saying that's bad, I just assumed by the pricing of the food this would be a higher standard type deal. The pricing doesn't match the ambience but no biggie, just saying.

I had a couple issues with my food. I would say my steak was under seasoned but honestly I just don't think it was seasoned at all. After adding salt on my own to it I somewhat saved it. They had no steak sauce, I just feel like if there is steak there should be steak sauce. And the mashed potatoes were pasty in texture. The only thing I really liked was the old fashion I got, but thats a standard drink.

Overall not worth the bill we paid for dinner.< /Text>

< review>
First impression when I walked in is that this was a very well run restaurant. The hostess was just so sweet. Our waiter was very charming and just felt like everyone there made an extra effort to make us comfortable.

I am an Agent in San Fernando with Farmers Insurnace and I had taken my father to the Farmers Insurance Open at Torry Pines. Their hospitality was so appreciated after our long day of walking around the golf course üòä

Food was stellar.

For our appetizer we started with a Selection of Fresh Seasonal Oysters with horse radish and 3 sauces. Perfect light weight starter and tasted delish.

Second we tried their most popular appetizer which was their Crispy Kurobuta Pork Belly Lollipops. They were full of flavor and defiantly our favorite.

For dinner I had their 18oz Bone-In Rib Eye Steak which was juicy, flavorful and filling. If you like steak this is the one to go with.

My Father had the Slow Braised Angus Beef Short-rib he loved.

Ambience was very relaxed, comfortable and Luxurious.<//review>

< Review>
A group of us ate here last night. So, let me start with the positives. The service I thought was really good. They seemed attentive and professional. The appetizers were good, we had the pork belly lollipops, and the foie gras (which was a special that night). Both were pretty good. My wife and I split the BOB salad, which I enjoyed.
The main course is where things went off the rails.  Overall the pace of the meal seemed kind of slow, but it seemed to take extra long to get the main dishes out. There were 6 of us, and 2 ordered the halibut special, and the rest ordered steak. There was a filet, two NY‚Äôs and the flat iron. Of the 4 steaks, only the flat iron came out warm. All the others came out cold. My in particular, which was one of the NY steaks, came out cold and undercooked, like way undercooked.  I ordered med-rare, and I got something that was undercooked for rare even. For sides we got the Mac and cheese, herb fries, and asparagus. Fries are in a cone, which makes it tough for sharing, Mac and cheese had a big blob of cheese melted on top, and was not very good.

We finally mentioned something towards the end, and the waiter tried to make things right by comping some deserts and appetizers.

With tip, we spent $250 a couple on that meal, which was painful for me, because I didn‚Äôt enjoy it.  Then to make matters worse, a few hours later, I got sick. I know I should have said something to the staff, but I don‚Äôt like to complain.

Bottom line, half the people enjoyed their dishes and the other half thought things were sub par. Frankly, I probably would have given 3 stars before I got sick, that put me off of this place forever. So my advice, eat here at your own risk.</Review>

I've made a mental note to try The Winery at UTC and finally got the chance to go. We didn't make any reservations and were not aware that we were supposed to on a Saturday evening so we didn't get a seat in the actual restaurant. However, there were open seating at the Winery Bar which was where we went. The bar had it's own patio and offered the same menu as the restaurant. We ordered a charcuterie board - variety of cheese, fruits, spreads, and meat. I only had one glass of Pinot Noir and a friend had a blood orange Bellini. Bellini was pretty refreshing. And my pinot was perfect for our charcuterie.

What made me like this place was probable the atmosphere. It was a little more on the casual side compared to the actual dine in restaurant. There were nice seats inside the bar, but we opted for the outside patio because it was just too perfect to be indoor. It was the evening and the lights on the trees made the place feel like I wasn't even at the mall anymore. UTC really turned itself around! Anyways, I had a great time and will definitely be back to the Winery Bar.

The waitress was nice and offered to get us more fruits from our board.< /text>

< Review>
This is a great spot if you have a short amount of time and you want some quality Shanghai food. Their dumplings are fair portions and made really well. It is very good but be cautious when biting into one because some of them are so juicy you could potentially get soup all over yourself. The service is fast and efficient and the staff is friendly. Parking can be tough so come early or come prepared.<//Review>

< user_id>
110288469148184652948<//user_id>
< Rate>
3</Rate>
<Pics>None< /Pics>< review>
You can't go to a place called Xiao Long Bao Kitchen and not order the aforementioned dish, so of course I had the xiao long bao along with the Shanghai boiled dumplings with shrimp. The XLB were juicy and all in tact, but the pork and soup inside lacked some flavor. The complementing vinegar sauce was delicious, with pieces of shredded ginger. The boiled pork and shrimp dumplings were large, but as with the XLBs, lacked some flavor. The accompanying sauce had a red tint to it, which made me think it was spicy, but I was pleasantly surprised. The sauce was without spice and delicious with the boiled dumplings. As with other traditional Chinese places, you can expect complementary tea with the meal, which was pretty affordable. $8 for 8 XLBs or 10 boiled dumplings!

This place was okay, but my top choice for dumplings in SSF will still be Dumpling Empire. Gave this place a try because Dumpling Empire is closed on Wednesdays and Kingdom of Dumpling in the Sunset seemed too far for my dumpling cravings.< /review>

<Time>1599952420515</Time>< Text>
One of my favorite Karaoke Bars in West LA, for sure. Unfortunately, do to Covid-19 there won't be Karaoke for a while. However, they do have outdoor seating available right now. I still enjoying going there because their entire staff is so friendly, prices are right, and the their food is so good! I have been going there for over 5 years and I honestly have nothing to complain about. If you're going to check out BW 11 (the local nickname) for the first time, keep in mind that you may need some patience to find parking if you're not going to take a Lyft or Uber. They are in a little corner plaza so the parking can be very limited from time to time. Lately because of the pandemic, it's been very easy to find parking.

Side note: When they do open back up to full capacity, you'll want to get there early to put you name on the list to sing, that place gets packed! Lol</Text>

< Review>
Boardwalk 11:

My husband and I were looking for a venue that offers fun, food and a good space to entertain our friends and family for an evening to celebrate his retirement and my birthday.

As usual, we went online, did a search for those types of TAGS and came across Boardwalk 11.

We looked at most of the 500+ reviews already posted, including the negative ones. Some of those are really serious: Cold old food, roaches, bad service, etc.

Most people may have been persuaded to not even consider this place, but we thought: Can it really be THAT BAD?

The answer is NO! ‚Äì We went the same day we did our research, parked in the parking lot (which is free valet [translation: If you eat or drink, incl. non-alcoholic drinks you only need to consider tipping the valet]), went inside and we started to look around.

The place was almost empty, but it was just a little after 6:30 PM on a Tuesday. There was a clear friendliness between patrons, bartender, server and newcomers like us.

We sat down near the bar, got a menu and were surprised about the prices as those are pretty competitive to other places.

Even though we felt ‚Äúadventurous‚Äù, both of us ended up with the same dish: BBQ Chicken Tostada Salad. The shell was crispy, the salad fresh and the chicken tender. ‚Äì It was good.

Still, having some of those negative reviews in mind, I kept looking for anything that would gross me out. I didn‚Äôt see anything. No Roaches, no bugs of any kind. In fact, the entire place was clean, inviting, and fun.

Our server also managed to bring the owner over to us. Which was nice, as I kept thinking about the negative review he got and I expected to meet a grumpy, old, unkempt, mean, horrid person. He is not.

Steve introduced himself and started chatting with us about the venue. He is open minded, courteous, and funny.

Even though things may change in the future, but for right now, and based on our first impression, we are looking forward to our little celebration at Boardwalk 11.<//Review>

< Review>
I've walked past this place like a million times but never went in until just recently.  Imagine my surprise when I saw how clean, intimate and classy the establishment was.  It's a perfect place to bring a date or a small group of friends for local craft beer, good food and watching people sing their favorite karaoke songs.  I would definitely recommend this restaurant-bar to others and would come back again.  I knocked off a star due to it's utter lack of parking.  However, for those who happen to live in the area, it is the quintessential neighborhood bar experience and would encourage others in the Palms area to check it out.  A perfect venue for a date.</Review>

< name>
Sean Dennison</name>
< review>
I went here to enjoy a karaoke night with a new friend and got a table near the karaoke host and close to the stage. The place itself was nice enough. Lots of comfortable seating. Good sound system. Nice branded stage with good lighting. They had a charging station but I ended up grabbing an outlet closer to my table to charge my phone.

It was St. Patrick's Day so my friend and I both ordered green beers which were featured on the menu. Basically they were green versions of Miller Light which worked for us.

We both put songs in with the karaoke host immediately upon arrival and settled in at our table to look through the karaoke book with our green beers. It was posted that we could only put one song in at a time so that's what we did. I was told the wait to sing was about an hour and a half. Not being terribly long we patiently waited our turns while being entertained by the other performers.

Two and a half hours and four beers later my friend and I had still not been invited up to sing yet and I would soon have to head home to get some sleep for work the next day so I asked the karaoke host again if he could work us into the lineup soon. He said we were 7 songs away.  That would be another half an hour! 3 hours wait to sing one song??!! Which would have been twice his original estimate of one and a half hours. That was ridiculous and not ok.

Now mind you I watched certain performers get up there 2 or three times throughout the night while we waited to sing once. I am certain that the karaoke hosts math was not off when he gave the earlier time estimate but seemed to not value our time or have any integrity whatsoever and just put others before us time after time after time to add another 1.5 hours of singers between our first songs.

In the end I paid the bill and left after waiting 2.5 hours. Very dissatisfied.< /review>

< text>
I'm so sad.. I love to support local small dive bars, and this spot is super awesome. But tonight,.First of all, the prices are a little steep for what kind of bar this is.  It's a dumpy bar in a strip mall in the middle of Palms - everything should be cheap, but it's not.  I haven't been there lately, but they used to have a two drink minimum on weekend nights.  If you're not careful with what you order, those two things can add up to a pretty serious tab.

Second, I personally think the crowd here is pretty annoying.  I know people love that there are "regulars" here, but I kind of get tired of seeing the same people sing the same stuff every time I'm there.  The big groups that come here e.g. offices parties or bachelorette parties (the worst) can get quite annoying.  Although, this is probably not something unique to Boardwalk 11.

But, the main problem with this place is that on the weekend, the wait can easily be two hours (I've seen longer).  It's kind of tough to sit through people butchering songs for 2+ hours just so you can finally get your one song in.  Also, as I think maybe someone alluded to, the big groups that are there seemingly never have a problem getting their songs in.  Based on what I've seen, I think it's pretty safe to say that there's some shenanigans going on with the waiting list< /text>
